)@@G@@@@@@@=@@@@@ @@@@@#@@@@@^*[S@@@*SDFF*@ @@@@PRTT 3R1 - USER'S GUIDE       EV
)@@G@@@#@@@@1INTRODUCTION     @G@@@@      PRTT IS A PROCESSOR THAT CAN BE USEDEW
)@@G@@ TO LIST INFORMATION ABOUT ALL@H@@@@ OR SOME OF THE ELEMENTS IN A PROGRAEX
)@@G@@M FILE.  IT IS SIMILAR TO THE STANDARD    @G@@@@ UNIVAC (@PRT,T) BUT IT EY
)@@G@@IS MORE FLEXIBLE AND PRODUCES A MORE COMPACT    @G@@@@ LISTING.  PRTT ISEZ
)@@G@@ NORMALLY USED FROM DEMAND, BUT IT CAN BE USED FROM   @#@@@@ BATCH IF DEFA
)@@G@@SIRED.@[@@@@SPACE @B@@@@      THE PROCESSOR CALL IS AS FOLLOWS:   @[@@@@FB
)@@G@@SPACE @C@@@@  @PRTT<,OPTIONS>  <SPEC1><,SPEC2>,...<,SPEC-N> @[@@@@SPACE FC
)@@G@@@G@@@@      EACH SPECIFICATION TAKES THE STANDARD FORM OF:  Q*F(C)/R.E/VFD
)@@G@@   .  @G@@@@ ALL PARAMETERS ARE OPTIONAL.  IF NO FILE IS SPECIFIED, TPF$FE
)@@G@@ IS ASSUMED.@ @@@@ FILE CONTINUATION IS ALLOWED.@]@@@@1BASIC USAGE@G@@@@FF
)@@G@@      IF ONLY A FILE NAME (NO ELEMENT OR VERSION NAME) IS SPECIFIED,    FG
)@@G@@@G@@@@ ALL ELEMENTS IN THE FILE ARE ELIGIBLE FOR PRINTING, DEPENDING ON FH
)@@G@@TYPE  @H@@@@ SPECIFICATION OPTIONS.  IF AN ELEMENT NAME BUT NO VERSION NFI
)@@G@@AME IS GIVEN,     @G@@@@ ALL ELEMENTS WITH THAT NAME, REGARDLESS OF VERSFJ
)@@G@@ION, MAY BE PRINTED.    @G@@@@ THIS IS SIMILAR TO (@PRT,TV ./***********FK
)@@G@@*), BUT IS EASIER TO TYPE!    @G@@@@ IF ONLY A VERSION NAME IS SPECIFIEDFL
)@@G@@, ALL ELEMENTS WITH THAT VERSION MAY@G@@@@ BE LISTED.  IF BOTH ELEMENT AFM
)@@G@@ND VERSION NAME ARE GIVEN ON A SINGLE     @C@@@@ SPECIFICATION, BOTH MUSFN
)@@G@@T MATCH.  EXAMPLES:     @[@@@@SPACE @]@@@@COLUMN 7    @]@@@@  @PRTT A*B.FO
)@@G@@@C@@@@0     LISTS ALL UNDELETED ELEMENTS IN FILE A*B. @[@@@@SPACE @ @@@@FP
)@@G@@  @PRTT A*B.XYZ,ABS1./PROG2   @G@@@@0     LISTS ALL UNDELETED ELEMENTS WFQ
)@@G@@ITH ELEMENT NAME 'XYZ' IN FILE A*B, @G@@@@      AND ALL UNDELETED ELEMENFR
)@@G@@TS WITH VERSION NAME 'PROG2' IN FILE ABS1.@[@@@@SPACE @ @@@@  @PRTT A*B.FS
)@@G@@PROG1/A,.PROG3    @F@@@@0     LISTS ALL UNDELETED ELEMENTS WITH ELEMENT/FT
)@@G@@VERSION NAME OF   @E@@@@      'PROG1/A' OR ELEMENT NAME 'PROG3' (ANY VERFU
)@@G@@SION) IN    @#@@@@      FILE A*B.   @]@@@@SPACE 2     @]@@@@COLUMN 2    FV
)@@G@@@G@@@@      THERE ARE TWO SPECIAL OPTIONS WHICH AFFECT ELEMENT SPECIFICAFW
)@@G@@TION. @G@@@@ THE 'I' OPTION IS USED TO INVERT THE NORMAL ELEMENT/VERSIONFX
)@@G@@ MATCHING   @G@@@@ ALGORITHM.  WHEN THIS OPTION IS USED, ALL ELEMENTS BUFY
)@@G@@T THOSE WHICH ARE @G@@@@ SPECIFICALLY MATCHED ARE LISTED.  THE 'I' OPTIOFZ
)@@G@@N DOES NOT INVERT THE   @D@@@@ MEANING OF ANY OF THE TYPE SPECIFICATION GA
)@@G@@OPTIONS.    @E@@@@ THE 'Z' OPTION MAY BE USED TO SPECIFY ELEMENT CONTINUGB
)@@G@@ATION.@F@@@@ IF THIS OPTION IS GIVEN, ANY NULL ELEMENT/VERSION FIELD WILGC
)@@G@@L BE  @E@@@@ REPLACED WITH THE ONE WHICH PRECEDED IT.  EXAMPLES FOLLOW: GD
)@@G@@@[@@@@SPACE @]@@@@COLUMN 7    @A@@@@  @PRTT,I A*B.MAIN,PROGFILE./SPECIALGE
)@@G@@@G@@@@0     THIS LISTS ALL UNDELETED ELEMENTS IN FILE A*B EXCEPT THOSE WGF
)@@G@@ITH   @G@@@@      ELEMENT NAME 'MAIN' (REGARDLESS OF VERSION) AND ALL UNGG
)@@G@@DELETED     @G@@@@      ELEMENTS IN FILE PROGFILE EXCEPT THOSE WITH A VEGH
